SELECT t.vehicle_id, t.brand, t.change_date, t.description, t.license_plate, t.model, t.model_year, t.registration_date, t.renavan, t.situation, t.vehicle_type, t.year_manufacture, v0.vehicle_id, v0.url
FROM (
    SELECT v.vehicle_id, v.brand, v.change_date, v.description, v.license_plate, v.model, v.model_year, v.registration_date, v.renavan, v.situation, v.vehicle_type, v.year_manufacture
    FROM vehicles AS v
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN vehicle_image AS v0 ON t.vehicle_id = v0.vehicle_id
ORDER BY t.vehicle_id
